  function recalcClasses() {
    var width = root.clientWidth;
    var newSize = 'desktop';
    var newOrientation = (window.innerHeight > window.innerWidth) ? 'portrait' : 'landscape';
    if (width < 768) {
      newSize = 'phone';
    } else if (width < 992) {
      newSize = 'tablet';
    } else if (width > 1245) {
      newSize = 'wide';
    }
    if (size !== newSize) {
      root.classList.remove('html_' + size);
      root.classList.add('html_' + newSize);
      size = newSize;
      if (newSize === 'wide') {
        root.classList.add('widescreen');
        LMDA.isWidescreen = false;
      }
      LMDA.device.size = newSize;
    }

      root.classList.remove('html_' + currentOrientation);
      root.classList.add('html_' + newOrientation);
      currentOrientation = newOrientation;
      LMDA.device.orientation = newOrientation;
    }
  }

  function throttleOnResize() {
    if (!resizeTimeout) {
      resizeTimeout = setTimeout(function () {

        recalcClasses();
